D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, your own Rainy/Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): To use it, set Sync Service to Online Synchronization in preferences then provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  784): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  784): rainy.notesync.org - https://notesync.org:8080/[username]/[password]/
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Note: you might want to back up your Tomboy notes before syncing, since this app is still under development and may corrupt your Tomboy notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Please see http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the location of the *.note files on all platforms.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.

D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, your own Rainy/Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): To use it, set Sync Service to Online Synchronization in preferences then provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  784): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  784): rainy.notesync.org - https://notesync.org:8080/[username]/[password]/
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Note: you might want to back up your Tomboy notes before syncing, since this app is still under development and may corrupt your Tomboy notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Please see http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the location of the *.note files on all platforms.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Also, Tomdroid is always looking for new contributors. If you are interested join the tomdroid-dev team on Launchpad: http://launchpad.net/~tomdroid-dev.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  784): You have no notes here yet. To get started, set your Synchronization preferences under Settings. There are two synchronization options described below.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, your own Rainy/Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): To use it, set Sync Service to Online Synchronization in preferences then provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  784): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  784): rainy.notesync.org - https://notesync.org:8080/[username]/[password]/
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Note: you might want to back up your Tomboy notes before syncing, since this app is still under development and may corrupt your Tomboy notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Please see http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the location of the *.note files on all platforms.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Also, Tomdroid is always looking for new contributors. If you are interested join the tomdroid-dev team on Launchpad: http://launchpad.net/~tomdroid-dev.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Lastly, if you encounter any issue, please report it at: https://bugs.launchpad.net/tomdroid

D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, your own Rainy/Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): To use it, set Sync Service to Online Synchronization in preferences then provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  784): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  784): rainy.notesync.org - https://notesync.org:8080/[username]/[password]/
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Note: you might want to back up your Tomboy notes before syncing, since this app is still under development and may corrupt your Tomboy notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Please see http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the location of the *.note files on all platforms.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.

D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.

D/nofatclips(  784): You have no notes here yet. To get started, set your Synchronization preferences under Settings. There are two synchronization options described below.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization
D/nofatclips(  784): Online Synchronization is what you are looking for if you want to sync to Tomboy-Online, your own Rainy/Snowy server or any server supporting the Tomboy Web REST API.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): To use it, set Sync Service to Online Synchronization in preferences then provide a Server URL. Here are some of the public ones:
D/nofatclips(  784): Tomboy Online - https://edge.tomboy-online.org/
D/nofatclips(  784): rainy.notesync.org - https://notesync.org:8080/[username]/[password]/
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Once set, hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar to synchronize your notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Note: you might want to back up your Tomboy notes before syncing, since this app is still under development and may corrupt your Tomboy notes.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): Please see http://live.gnome.org/Tomboy/Directories for the location of the *.note files on all platforms.
D/nofatclips(  784): 
D/nofatclips(  784): SD Card
D/nofatclips(  784): Put your Tomboy notes (*.note) on your SD Card under tomdroid/. Once the notes are copied, set Sync Service to SD Card in preferences then hit the Sync logo on Tomdroid's top bar.
